For each graph node that has all parents written to topology, calls `streamGraphNode.writeToTopology(internalTopologyBuilder)`\\n5. Validates copartition and checks unprovideed names\\n\\n### Stage 2: Graph Node to InternalTopologyBuilder Conversion\\n**File:** `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/graph/GraphNode.java`\\n\\nEach GraphNode type implements the abstract method `writeToTopology(InternalTopologyBuilder topologyBuilder)`. This converts the logical graph representation into physical topology builders:\\n- `StreamSourceNode` calls `topologyBuilder.addSource()`\\n- `ProcessorGraphNode` calls `processorParameters.addProcessorTo(topologyBuilder, ...)`\\n- `StateStoreNode` calls `topologyBuilder.addStateStore(storeBuilder)`\\n- `SinkNode` writes sink processors to the topology\\n\\n### Stage 3: InternalTopologyBuilder - Node Factory Registration\\n**File:** `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/internals/InternalTopologyBuilder.java`\\n\\nThe InternalTopologyBuilder maintains:\\n- `private final Map<String, NodeFactory<?, ?, ?, ?>> nodeFactories` - registered node factories\\n- `private final Map<String, StoreFactory> stateFactories` - registered state store factories\\n- `private final Map<String, String> storeToChangelogTopic` - changelog topic mappings\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- `addProcessor(String name, ProcessorSupplier supplier, String... parents)` - registers processor nodes\\n- `addSource(String name, String... topics)` - registers source nodes\\n- `addStateStore(StoreBuilder<?> storeBuilder, String... processorNames)` - registers state stores by wrapping with StoreBuilderWrapper\\n\\n### Stage 4: State Store Registration\\n**File:** `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/internals/InternalTopologyBuilder.java` (lines 591-627)\\n\\nState stores are registered through `addStateStore()`:\\n1. Calls `topology.sources()` to initialize source node latency tracking\\n\\n### Key Data Structures\\n\\n**ProcessorNode:** Represents an executable processor in the topology graph, connected via parent-child relationships\\n\\n**SourceNode:** Represents a source of data from a Kafka topic\\n\\n**SinkNode:** Represents a sink that writes to a Kafka topic\\n\\n**StateStore:** Created from StoreFactory via the builder pattern, with changelog topics tracked for fault tolerance\\n\\n**ProcessorTopology:** The compiled physical topology containing all nodes, stores, and topic mappings ready for execution\\n\\n### Call Chain Summary\\n\\n1. `StreamsBuilder.build(Properties)` \\n2. → `InternalStreamsBuilder.buildAndOptimizeTopology(Properties)`\\n3. → For each GraphNode: `GraphNode.writeToTopology(InternalTopologyBuilder)`\\n4. → `InternalTopologyBuilder.addProcessor()` / `addSource()` / `addStateStore()`\\n5. → `InternalTopologyBuilder.buildTopology()`\\n6. → `InternalTopologyBuilder.build(Set<String> nodeGroup)`\\n7. → For each NodeFactory: `factory.build()` and connection methods\\n8. → `buildProcessorNode()` - This converts the logical graph representation into physical topology builders:\\n- `StreamSourceNode` calls `topologyBuilder.addSource()`\\n- `ProcessorGraphNode` calls `processorParameters.addProcessorTo(topologyBuilder, ...)`\\n- `StateStoreNode` calls `topologyBuilder.addStateStore(storeBuilder)`\\n- `SinkNode` writes sink processors to the topology\\n\\n### Stage 3: InternalTopologyBuilder - Node Factory Registration\\n**File:** `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/internals/InternalTopologyBuilder.java`\\n\\nThe InternalTopologyBuilder maintains:\\n- `private final Map<String, NodeFactory<?, ?, ?, ?>> nodeFactories` - registered node factories\\n- `private final Map<String, StoreFactory> stateFactories` - registered state store factories\\n- `private final Map<String, String> storeToChangelogTopic` - changelog topic mappings\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- `addProcessor(String name, ProcessorSupplier supplier, String... parents)` - registers processor nodes\\n- `addSource(String name, String... topics)` - registers source nodes\\n- `addStateStore(StoreBuilder<?> storeBuilder, String... processorNames)` - registers state stores by wrapping with StoreBuilderWrapper\\n\\n### Stage 4: State Store Registration\\n**File:** `streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/internals/InternalTopologyBuilder.java` (lines 591-627)\\n\\nState stores are registered through `addStateStore()`:\\n1. Calls `topology.sources()` to initialize source node latency tracking\\n\\n### Key Data Structures\\n\\n**ProcessorNode:** Represents an executable processor in the topology graph, connected via parent-child relationships\\n\\n**SourceNode:** Represents a source of data from a Kafka topic\\n\\n**SinkNode:** Represents a sink that writes to a Kafka topic\\n\\n**StateStore:** Created from StoreFactory via the builder pattern, with changelog topics tracked for fault tolerance\\n\\n**ProcessorTopology:** The compiled physical topology containing all nodes, stores, and topic mappings ready for execution\\n\\n### Call Chain Summary\\n\\n1. `StreamsBuilder.build(Properties)` \\n2. → `InternalStreamsBuilder.buildAndOptimizeTopology(Properties)`\\n3. → For each GraphNode: `GraphNode.writeToTopology(InternalTopologyBuilder)`\\n4. → `InternalTopologyBuilder.addProcessor()` / `addSource()` / `addStateStore()`\\n5. → `InternalTopologyBuilder.buildTopology()`\\n6. → `InternalTopologyBuilder.build(Set<String> nodeGroup)`\\n7. → For each NodeFactory: `factory.build()` and connection methods\\n8. → `buildProcessorNode()` - builds state stores via `StoreFactory.builder().build()`\\n9. → Creates `ProcessorTopology` with all compiled nodes\\n10. → `StreamTask` receives ProcessorTopology in constructor and initializes execution context\\n\\nThis architecture separates concerns: the high-level DSL (StreamsBuilder), logical topology graph (GraphNode), topology builder (InternalTopologyBuilder), and the compiled physical topology (ProcessorTopology) ready for execution by StreamTask instances.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
